Breaking Changes Addressed:
  • upload-artifact v6: Now uses Node.js 24
  • download-artifact v7: Now uses Node.js 24
  • download-artifact v4+: Artifacts are immutable, using pattern + merge-multiple
  • setup-java v5: Added 'distribution' parameter (using temurin)

Workflow Behavior:
  • ci.yml: Runs on every push/PR (build + test only)
  • build.yml: Creates 'dev' pre-release on push to main branches
  • release.yml: Creates stable release on git tags (v*)

To apply changes:
  git add .github/
  git commit -m 'Update GitHub Actions to latest versions'
  git push
